--- Research Result 2 ---
Based on the search results, here's a summary of the limitations of using pre-built FlutterFlow templates for booking apps, especially concerning customization and scalability:

**Customization Limitations:**

*   **Limited Flexibility:** FlutterFlow templates offer pre-built components, which can restrict deep UI and backend customization.
